**Speed** is defined as the **rate at which an object covers distance**, so mathematically:  

\[
\text{Speed} = \frac{\text{Distance}}{\text{Time}}
\]  

- **Distance** = how far something travels  
- **Time** = how long it takes  
- **Speed** = distance covered per unit of time  

For example:  
- If a car travels 120 km in 2 hours, its speed is \( 120 Ã· 2 = 60 \text{ km/h} \).  

You want me to also cover **the rearrangements** for finding Distance or Time?
